\DoxyCodeLine{00060     \textcolor{keyword}{explicit} CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT(}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061         FLOAT topLeftX,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062         FLOAT topLeftY,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063         FLOAT width,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064         FLOAT height,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065         FLOAT minDepth = D3D12\_MIN\_DEPTH,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH )}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068         TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069         TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070         Width = width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071         Height = height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075     \textcolor{keyword}{explicit} CD3DX12\_VIEWPORT(}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076         \_In\_ ID3D12Resource* pResource,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077         UINT mipSlice = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078         FLOAT topLeftX = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079         FLOAT topLeftY = 0.0f,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080         FLOAT minDepth = D3D12\_MIN\_DEPTH,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081         FLOAT maxDepth = D3D12\_MAX\_DEPTH )}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} Desc = pResource-\/>GetDesc();}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceWidth = Desc.Width >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085         \textcolor{keyword}{const} UINT64 SubresourceHeight = Desc.Height >> mipSlice;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (Desc.Dimension)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_BUFFER:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091             Width = Desc.Width -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE1D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096             TopLeftY = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? SubresourceWidth : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098             Height = 1.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE2D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} D3D12\_RESOURCE\_DIMENSION\_TEXTURE3D:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102             TopLeftX = topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103             TopLeftY = topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104             Width = (SubresourceWidth ? SubresourceWidth : 1.0f) -\/ topLeftX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105             Height = (SubresourceHeight ? SubresourceHeight: 1.0f) -\/ topLeftY;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{00110         MinDepth = minDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111         MaxDepth = maxDepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{01684 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} UINT D3D12CalcSubresource( UINT MipSlice, UINT ArraySlice, UINT PlaneSlice, UINT MipLevels, UINT ArraySize )}
\DoxyCodeLine{01685 \{ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01686     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} MipSlice + ArraySlice * MipLevels + PlaneSlice * MipLevels * ArraySize; }

\DoxyCodeLine{01910         RequiredSize > SIZE\_T(-\/1) || }

\DoxyCodeLine{01912             (FirstSubresource != 0 || NumSubresources != 1)))}

\DoxyCodeLine{01915     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01920     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01921         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01922     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01923     }
\DoxyCodeLine{01924     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (UINT i = 0; i < NumSubresources; ++i)}

\DoxyCodeLine{01926         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pRowSizesInBytes[i] > SIZE\_T(-\/1)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{01936     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01937     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01938     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01939         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (UINT i = 0; i < NumSubresources; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{01940         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01941             CD3DX12\_TEXTURE\_COPY\_LOCATION Dst(pDestinationResource, i + FirstSubresource);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01942             CD3DX12\_TEXTURE\_COPY\_LOCATION Src(pIntermediate, pLayouts[i]);}

\DoxyCodeLine{02703 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02704 \textcolor{comment}{// D3DX12 State Object Creation Helpers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02705 \textcolor{comment}{// }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02706 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper classes for creating new style state objects out of an arbitrary set of subobjects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02707 \textcolor{comment}{// Uses STL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02708 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02709 \textcolor{comment}{// Start by instantiating CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC (see it's public methods).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02710 \textcolor{comment}{// One of its methods is CreateSubobject(), which has a comment showing a couple of options for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02711 \textcolor{comment}{// defining subobjects using the helper classes for each subobject (CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02712 \textcolor{comment}{// etc.). The subobject helpers each have methods specific to the subobject for configuring it's }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02713 \textcolor{comment}{// contents.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02714 \textcolor{comment}{// }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02715 \textcolor{comment}{//================================================================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02744             Iter != m\_SubobjectList.end(); Iter++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02745         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02746             m\_SubobjectArray.push\_back(*Iter);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02747             \textcolor{comment}{// Store new location in array so we can redirect pointers contained in subobjects }}

\DoxyCodeLine{02775 }
\DoxyCodeLine{02776     \textcolor{comment}{// CreateSubobject creates a sububject helper (e.g. CD3DX12\_HIT\_GROUP\_SUBOBJECT) }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02777     \textcolor{comment}{// whose lifetime is owned by this class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02778     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02779     \textcolor{comment}{// }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02780     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC Collection1(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_COLLECTION);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02781     \textcolor{comment}{//    auto Lib0 = Collection1.CreateSubobject<CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT>();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02782     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[0]);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02783     \textcolor{comment}{//    Lib0-\/>DefineExport(L"{}rayGenShader0"{}); // in practice these export listings might be }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02784     \textcolor{comment}{//                                          // data/engine driven}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02785     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02786     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02787     \textcolor{comment}{// Alternatively, users can instantiate sububject helpers explicitly, such as via local }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02788     \textcolor{comment}{// variables instead, passing the state object desc that should point to it into the helper }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02789     \textcolor{comment}{// constructor (or call mySubobjectHelper.AddToStateObject(Collection1)).  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02790     \textcolor{comment}{// In this alternative scenario, the user must keep the subobject alive as long as the state }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02791     \textcolor{comment}{// object it is associated with is alive, else it's pointer references will be stale.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02792     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02793     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02794     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_DESC RaytracingState2(D3D12\_STATE\_OBJECT\_TYPE\_RAYTRACING\_PIPELINE);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02795     \textcolor{comment}{//    CD3DX12\_DXIL\_LIBRARY\_SUBOBJECT LibA(RaytracingState2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02796     \textcolor{comment}{//    LibA.SetDXILLibrary(\&pMyAppDxilLibs[4]); // not manually specifying exports }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02797     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // -\/ meaning all exports in the libraries }}
\DoxyCodeLine{02798     \textcolor{comment}{//                                             // are exported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02799     \textcolor{comment}{//    etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02800 }
\DoxyCodeLine{02801     \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}

\DoxyCodeLine{02806         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pSubobject;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02807     \}}
